bug-reports 2020-03-26 01:09:25 If you have too many wings, or move too quickly with wings, they spaz out and glitch your plane to the far lands and out of existance.
Speculation: The wing panel lift equation might cause a positive feedback loop, where if there are enough wings, or going fast enough, it causes the wing to spaz, which would be seen as a lot of momentum, causing the wings to lift in the opposite direction, this time with more force due to the massive momentum, and so on and so forth.
If this is the case, then you could fix this by making the lift function not go above a certain limit, easiest way to do this is with a non linear function. My suggestion: Sigmoid[1/(1+2[the higher this is, the faster it will change while approaching 0]^-x)]
